[30;1m1703 | [0m[35m        - Fisheye model directly applies radial distortion[0m
[30;1m1704 | [0m[35m        - Both models use shift_limit to control distortion center[0m
[30;1m1705 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m1706 | [0m[35m    Example:[0m
[30;1m1707 | [0m[35m        >>> import albumentations as A[0m

[30;1m1623 | [0m[35m    Note:[0m
[30;1m1624 | [0m[35m        - The transform first converts the input RGB image to the HSV color space.[0m
[30;1m1625 | [0m[35m        - Each channel (Hue, Saturation, Value) is adjusted independently.[0m

[30;1m1628 | [0m[35m        - This transform is particularly useful for color augmentation and simulating[0m
[30;1m1629 | [0m[35m          different lighting conditions.[0m
